Hey new-projects!

As a native engineer, I often find our API to be really difficult. We don't
have API documentation for the internal APIs that power much of the useful
user-personalization functionality on our website. I know that there must
be API endpoints for the stuff, but since the documentation doesn't exist,
it's prohibitively difficult to learn about what features we might add to
our native app. As a non-webapp engineer, when I need to look up an API, I
have to resort to spelunking around the unfamiliar webapp codebase.

The overall result: our native app doesn't sync with our website, so the
app feels stale and less personal.

So! Let's fix this! *As our team grows, it's important that we have some
shared API documentation.*

https://drive.google.com/open?id=1YqKBNjWt70uSwD8DO1peWN-qsmuLyacQfPle-XS4edo
https://drive.google.com/open?foo=bar&id=1YqKBNjWt70uSwD8DO1peWN-qsmuLyacQfPle-XS4ed1
https://drive.google.com/open?noid=1YqKBNjWt70uSwD8DO1peWN-qsmuLyacQfPle-XS4eX

*Note: This is maybe more like a "project request" since it needs help from
an API developer. (I'm happy to help out in whatever way possible, but I'm
not a webapp wizard yet - though I hope to be by the end of the project!).*

Ideally, we'll end up with API documentation so accessible, even a
caricature cartoon chef will find it delectable.

[image: Inline image 1]

<3,
Bryan

-- 
Bryan Clark
bryan@khanacademy.org

--001a11444b061ed5cf0536fcdbea
